2018-07-02 13:54:01 S√°ndor Fekete: Description:

Every time the frontend developers introduce the usage of a new routing, it needs to be implemented manually, and the classes must be generated again. We plan to avoid this by introducing a new function to the system. 

There will be a form somewhere, where this generation can be carried accord to the given/selected names/values. 

Developer fills the form with the desired values, and clicks on 'Generate'.

After this the routing_generator.php file takes over. 

It will create the desired record in the routing.php, if it doesnt exit. 

It will create the Controller file and in the Controller file, the doAction method. 

In case JSON response was selected, it will return a JSON file, according to the incoming parameter. In case DO was chosen and the name of the DO was given, it will create the DO file as well. 

After this process was successfully, the generate_class_list file will be run. 

A feedback will be displayed on the site, wheather the process was successful or not.
